        name: Joi.string().required(),

        password: Joi.string().required(),
      }),
    }),
    async (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction) =&gt; {
      const logger:Logger = Container.get('logger');
      logger.debug('Calling Sign-Up endpoint with body: %o', req.body );
      try {
        const authServiceInstance = Container.get(AuthService);
        const { user, token } = await authServiceInstance.SignUp(req.body as IUserInputDTO);
        return res.status(201).json({ user, token });
      } catch (e) {
        logger.error('ğŸ”¥ error: %o', e);
        return next(e);
      }
    },
  );

class UserResponse {

    private Long userId;
    private String name;
    //responseì— í•„ìš”í•œ fieldë“¤...
   

    public static userResponse of(UserResponse user){
             return new UserResponse (
                user.getuser().getuserId(),
                user.getName(),
               //responseì— í•„ìš”í•œ fieldë“¤...
    }

    public static List&lt;userResponse&gt; listOf(List&lt;User&gt; users) {
        return users.stream()
                .map(userResponse::of)
                .collect(Collectors.toList());
    }
}

            let result = await userService.save(req.body);
            res.send(result);
        } catch(err) {
            res.status(403).send(err);
        }
    }
};

### index
GET <http://localhost:3000> HTTP/1.1

### signUp
POST <http://localhost:3000/user> HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json

{
    "serviceNumber": "12345",
    "password": "1234"

}

### login
POST <http://localhost:3000/login> HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json

{
    "serviceNumber": "12345",
    "password": "1234"

}

### update user
PUT <http://localhost:3000/user/614ef30ad99cdc1c5b556301> HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json

{
    "name": "he"

}

### delete user
DELETE <http://localhost:3000/user/614ef30ad99cdc1c5b556301> HTTP/1.1

async function isItemEditor(loginUserId, targetItemId) {
    const user =  await userService.findOne({_id:loginUserId}, {group:true})
            .catch(err =&gt; {throw err});
    const targetItem = await itemService.read({_id: targetItemId}, {owner: true, contributors: true, accessGroups: true})
            .catch(err =&gt; {throw err});

    let isOwner = false, isContributor = false, isEditAccessGroup = false;
    try {
        isOwner = targetItem.owner._id === loginUserId;
    }catch(err) {
    }
    try {
        isContributor = targetItem.contributors.includes(loginUserId);
    }catch(err) {
    }
    try {
        isEditAccessGroup = accessGroups.edit.includes(user.group);
    }catch(err) {
    }

    return isOwner || isContributor || isEditAccessGroup;

}
